## nature-lang/nature

> [!info]
> â­ 2,246 Â· C Â· 2026-02-27  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/nature-lang/nature) Â· [Website](https://nature-lang.org)  
> `#System Programming Language` `#Self-developed Compiler` `#High-performance Runtime` `#Coroutine Implementation` `#c` `#compiler` `#hacktoberfest` `#lang` `#language` `#nature` `#programming-language` 
> Nature is a general-purpose system programming language and compiler implemented in pure C without LLVM dependency. It features a lightweight consistent syntax, strong static typing, memory safety, and exception handling. The language includes built-in concurrency primitives (go/future/channel/select), generics, enums, tagged unions, and advanced type system. Its runtime delivers high-performance GC with minimal STW, tcmalloc-style allocator, millions of coroutine switches per second, and libuv-based IO. Compiled binaries use musl libc static linking for cross-platform deployment.
> <sub>The Nature Programming Language</sub>

## beanshell/beanshell

> [!info]
> â­ 927 Â· Java Â· 2024-08-17  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/beanshell/beanshell)  
> `#Java Interpreter` `#Scripting Language` `#Embeddable` `#Dynamic Java` `#beanshell` `#beanshell-scripting-language` `#java` `#java-interpreter` `#java-shell` `#scripting-language` 
> BeanShell is a lightweight scripting language interpreter written entirely in Java, embeddable or standalone. It dynamically executes standard Java syntax with scripting extensions including loose types, commands, and method closures. Widely used for rapid prototyping, application extensibility, rules engines, configuration, and dynamic deployment. The next major release is 3.0.
> <sub>Beanshell scripting language</sub>

Fully compatible with InfluxDB 1.x/2.x write APIs and InfluxQL, while offering SQL queries via FlightSQL and HTTP. Ideal for monitoring, IoT sensors, financial analytics, and real-time dashboards.
> <sub>Scalable datastore for metrics, events, and real-time analytics</sub>

> Ceph is an open-source unified distributed storage system that provides object, block, and file storage through a single platform. It uses the CRUSH algorithm for autonomous data distribution with replication and erasure coding, delivering self-managing, self-healing capabilities and high availability. The system is designed for scale-out architecture, enabling horizontal scaling across commodity hardware while maintaining data consistency and fault tolerance. It is widely deployed in cloud computing platforms, Kubernetes persistent volumes, container storage, and enterprise data centers for mission-critical workloads.
> <sub>Ceph is a distributed object, block, and file storage platform</sub>

> This is an unofficial backport tool enabling Windows Subsystem for Android (originally for Windows 11) to run on Windows 10.
